DETECTOR   (TELES,SILI,SCIN) The multiplicity array, just outside C302400100012 
           the scattering chamber, consisted of 80 plastic        C302400100013 
           scintillator paddies. The paddies were 6.4 mm thick andC302400100014 
           were arranged in four azimuthal rings. The special     C302400100015 
           deltaE-E-Erej detector system was developed to measure C302400100016 
           stopped particles up to a proton energy of 200 MeV. TheC302400100017 
           deltaE detectors consisted of a 150 mu-m Si(P) and a   C302400100018 
           5-mm Si(Li). The rejection detector Erej was a large   C302400100019 
           area Si(Li). All three detectors were cooled to -30 C  C302400100020 
           by an external circulating refrigerated bath.          C302400100021 
           Intrinsic germanium detectors were developed for E     C302400100022 
           counters and were aligned so that the particles enteredC302400100023 
           the crystal perpendicular to their field lines.        C302400100024 
SAMPLE     The targets were 2.5 cm high by 5 cm wide. The targets C302400100025 
           were placed at 45 degrees with respect to the beam.    C302400100026 
           All the targets were supported on their edges with     C302400100027 
           1 mg/cm2 Mylar film in a plastic frame.                C302400100028 
CORRECTION Corrections were applied for the loss of particles due C302400100029 
           to reactions while stopping and for scattering out fromC302400100030 
           the detectors.                                         C302400100031
